Title: Bank of Maharashtra - Personal Loan for Salaried customers

--- TABLE 1 (TSV) ---
Particulars Scheme guidelines 1 Name of the scheme MAHA BANK PERSONAL LOAN SCHEME- for Salaried customers 2 Type of Facility Term Loan 3 Purpose of loan To cater to the requirements of meeting personal expenses. 4 Eligibility Borrowers are categorized in three category based on employment. Category –A. – Confirmed Employees of Central Govt. / State Govt. / Public Sector Undertakings/ Govt. Educational Institutions having Salary Account with BOM or any other Bank. Satisfactory account relationship with our Bank or any other Bank. Category –B. – Confirmed Employees of Private / Public Limited Company having external rating “A” & above having Salary Account with BOM or any other Bank. Satisfactory salary account relationship with Bank for at least -6- months. Category C. – Other Salary account holders (Confirmed Employees) whose salary is credited in our Bank and tie up arrangement with employer or irrevocable undertaking from employer is available. 5 Min Annual Income Minimum annual Income – 3.00 Lakhs. Minimum past 1 year ITR/Form 16 is Mandatory from current employer. 6 Maximum Quantum of Finance Maximum Rs 20.00 Lakhs. Loan amount is 20 times of Gross Monthly Income or as per Maximum Quantum of Finance whichever is lower. 7 Margin Nil 8 Age Limit Minimum: : 21 Years Maximum: 58 Years at the time of sanction Age of Borrower plus repayment period should not exceed retirement age or 60 years of age, whichever is lower. 9 Repayment Period For Category A Salary Account with Bank of Maharashtra - 84 months Salary Account with Other Bank - 60 months For Category B & C 60 months 10 Rate of Interest Click here to view the Interest Rate 11 Deduction For Category A Not to Exceed 65% of the Gross Monthly Income including Proposed EMI. For Category B & C Not to Exceed 60% of the Gross Monthly Income including Proposed EMI. 12 Security Nil (Clean Loan) 13 Guarantor Not required 14 Processing Fee 1.00 % of the loan amount + GST (Min: Rs 1000/-) 15 Documentation charge 0.20% of the loan amount + GST	Particulars Scheme guidelines 1 Name of the scheme MAHA BANK PERSONAL LOAN SCHEME- for Salaried customers 2 Type of Facility Term Loan 3 Purpose of loan To cater to the requirements of meeting personal expenses. 4 Eligibility Borrowers are categorized in three category based on employment. 1 Name of the scheme MAHA BANK PERSONAL LOAN SCHEME- for Salaried customers 2 Type of Facility Term Loan 3 Purpose of loan To cater to the requirements of meeting personal expenses. 4 Eligibility Borrowers are categorized in three category based on employment. Category –A. – Confirmed Employees of Central Govt. / State Govt. / Public Sector Undertakings/ Govt. Educational Institutions having Salary Account with BOM or any other Bank. Satisfactory account relationship with our Bank or any other Bank. Category –B. – Confirmed Employees of Private / Public Limited Company having external rating “A” & above having Salary Account with BOM or any other Bank. Satisfactory salary account relationship with Bank for at least -6- months. Category C. – Other Salary account holders (Confirmed Employees) whose salary is credited in our Bank and tie up arrangement with employer or irrevocable undertaking from employer is available. 5 Min Annual Income Minimum annual Income – 3.00 Lakhs. Minimum past 1 year ITR/Form 16 is Mandatory from current employer. 6 Maximum Quantum of Finance Maximum Rs 20.00 Lakhs. Loan amount is 20 times of Gross Monthly Income or as per Maximum Quantum of Finance whichever is lower. 7 Margin Nil 8 Age Limit Minimum: : 21 Years Maximum: 58 Years at the time of sanction Age of Borrower plus repayment period should not exceed retirement age or 60 years of age, whichever is lower. 9 Repayment Period For Category A Salary Account with Bank of Maharashtra - 84 months Salary Account with Other Bank - 60 months For Category B & C 60 months 10 Rate of Interest Click here to view the Interest Rate 11 Deduction For Category A Not to Exceed 65% of the Gross Monthly Income including Proposed EMI. Category –A. – Confirmed Employees of Central Govt. / State Govt. / Public Sector Undertakings/ Govt. Educational Institutions having Salary Account with BOM or any other Bank. Satisfactory account relationship with our Bank or any other Bank. Category –B. – Confirmed Employees of Private / Public Limited Company having external rating “A” & above having Salary Account with BOM or any other Bank. Satisfactory salary account relationship with Bank for at least -6- months. Category C. – Other Salary account holders (Confirmed Employees) whose salary is credited in our Bank and tie up arrangement with employer or irrevocable undertaking from employer is available. 5 Min Annual Income Minimum annual Income – 3.00 Lakhs. 3 Purpose of loan To cater to the requirements of meeting personal expenses. 4 Eligibility Borrowers are categorized in three category based on employment. Category –A. – Confirmed Employees of Central Govt. / State Govt. / Public Sector Undertakings/ Govt. Educational Institutions having Salary Account with BOM or any other Bank. Satisfactory account relationship with our Bank or any other Bank. Category –B. – Confirmed Employees of Private / Public Limited Company having external rating “A” & above having Salary Account with BOM or any other Bank. Satisfactory salary account relationship with Bank for at least -6- months. Category C. – Other Salary account holders (Confirmed Employees) whose salary is credited in our Bank and tie up arrangement with employer or irrevocable undertaking from employer is available. 5 Min Annual Income Minimum annual Income – 3.00 Lakhs. Minimum past 1 year ITR/Form 16 is Mandatory from current employer. 6 Maximum Quantum of Finance Maximum Rs 20.00 Lakhs. Loan amount is 20 times of Gross Monthly Income or as per Maximum Quantum of Finance whichever is lower. 7 Margin Nil 8 Age Limit Minimum: : 21 Years Maximum: 58 Years at the time of sanction Age of Borrower plus repayment period should not exceed retirement age or 60 years of age, whichever is lower. 9 Repayment Period For Category A Salary Account with Bank of Maharashtra - 84 months Salary Account with Other Bank - 60 months For Category B & C 60 months 10 Rate of Interest Click here to view the Interest Rate 11 Deduction For Category A Not to Exceed 65% of the Gross Monthly Income including Proposed EMI. 4 Eligibility Borrowers are categorized in three category based on employment. Category –A. – Confirmed Employees of Central Govt. / State Govt. / Public Sector Undertakings/ Govt. Educational Institutions having Salary Account with BOM or any other Bank. Satisfactory account relationship with our Bank or any other Bank. Category –B. – Confirmed Employees of Private / Public Limited Company having external rating “A” & above having Salary Account with BOM or any other Bank. Satisfactory salary account relationship with Bank for at least -6- months. Category C. – Other Salary account holders (Confirmed Employees) whose salary is credited in our Bank and tie up arrangement with employer or irrevocable undertaking from employer is available. 5 Min Annual Income Minimum annual Income – 3.00 Lakhs. Minimum past 1 year ITR/Form 16 is Mandatory from current employer. 6 Maximum Quantum of Finance Maximum Rs 20.00 Lakhs. Loan amount is 20 times of Gross Monthly Income or as per Maximum Quantum of Finance whichever is lower. 7 Margin Nil 8 Age Limit Minimum: : 21 Years Maximum: 58 Years at the time of sanction Age of Borrower plus repayment period should not exceed retirement age or 60 years of age, whichever is lower. 9 Repayment Period For Category A Salary Account with Bank of Maharashtra - 84 months Salary Account with Other Bank - 60 months For Category B & C 60 months 10 Rate of Interest Click here to view the Interest Rate 11 Deduction For Category A Not to Exceed 65% of the Gross Monthly Income including Proposed EMI. === TABLE 1 (pretty) ===
Particulars Scheme guidelines 1 Name of the scheme MAHA BANK PERSONAL LOAN SCHEME- for Salaried customers 2 Type of Facility Term Loan 3 Purpose of loan To cater to the requirements of meeting personal expenses. 4 Eligibility Borrowers are categorized in three category based on employment. Category –A. – Confirmed Employees of Central Govt. / State Govt. / Public Sector Undertakings/ Govt. Educational Institutions having Salary Account with BOM or any other Bank. Satisfactory account relationship with our Bank or any other Bank. Category –B. – Confirmed Employees of Private / Public Limited Company having external rating “A” & above having Salary Account with BOM or any other Bank. Satisfactory salary account relationship with Bank for at least -6- months. 1 Name of the scheme MAHA BANK PERSONAL LOAN SCHEME- for Salaried customers 2 Type of Facility Term Loan 3 Purpose of loan To cater to the requirements of meeting personal expenses. 4 Eligibility Borrowers are categorized in three category based on employment. Category –A. – Confirmed Employees of Central Govt. / State Govt. / Public Sector Undertakings/ Govt. Educational Institutions having Salary Account with BOM or any other Bank. Satisfactory account relationship with our Bank or any other Bank. Category –B. – Confirmed Employees of Private / Public Limited Company having external rating “A” & above having Salary Account with BOM or any other Bank. Satisfactory salary account relationship with Bank for at least -6- months. Category C. – Other Salary account holders (Confirmed Employees) whose salary is credited in our Bank and tie up arrangement with employer or irrevocable undertaking from employer is available. 5 Min Annual Income Minimum annual Income – 3.00 Lakhs. Minimum past 1 year ITR/Form 16 is Mandatory from current employer. 6 Maximum Quantum of Finance Maximum Rs 20.00 Lakhs. Loan amount is 20 times of Gross Monthly Income or as per Maximum Quantum of Finance whichever is lower. 7 Margin Nil 8 Age Limit Minimum: : 21 Years Maximum: 58 Years at the time of sanction Age of Borrower plus repayment period should not exceed retirement age or 60 years of age, whichever is lower. 9 Repayment Period For Category A Salary Account with Bank of Maharashtra - 84 months Salary Account with Other Bank - 60 months For Category B & C 60 months 10 Rate of Interest Click here to view the Interest Rate 11 Deduction For Category A Not to Exceed 65% of the Gross Monthly Income including Proposed EMI. 2 Type of Facility Term Loan 3 Purpose of loan To cater to the requirements of meeting personal expenses. 4 Eligibility Borrowers are categorized in three category based on employment. Category –A. – Confirmed Employees of Central Govt. / State Govt. / Public Sector Undertakings/ Govt. Educational Institutions having Salary Account with BOM or any other Bank. Satisfactory account relationship with our Bank or any other Bank. Category –B. – Confirmed Employees of Private / Public Limited Company having external rating “A” & above having Salary Account with BOM or any other Bank. Satisfactory salary account relationship with Bank for at least -6- months. Category C. – Other Salary account holders (Confirmed Employees) whose salary is credited in our Bank and tie up arrangement with employer or irrevocable undertaking from employer is available. 5 Min Annual Income Minimum annual Income – 3.00 Lakhs. Minimum past 1 year ITR/Form 16 is Mandatory from current employer. 6 Maximum Quantum of Finance Maximum Rs 20.00 Lakhs. Loan amount is 20 times of Gross Monthly Income or as per Maximum Quantum of Finance whichever is lower. 7 Margin Nil 8 Age Limit Minimum: : 21 Years Maximum: 58 Years at the time of sanction Age of Borrower plus repayment period should not exceed retirement age or 60 years of age, whichever is lower. 9 Repayment Period For Category A Salary Account with Bank of Maharashtra - 84 months Salary Account with Other Bank - 60 months For Category B & C 60 months 10 Rate of Interest Click here to view the Interest Rate 11 Deduction For Category A Not to Exceed 65% of the Gross Monthly Income including Proposed EMI. Loan amount is 20 times of Gross Monthly Income or as per Maximum Quantum of Finance whichever is lower. 7 Margin Nil 8 Age Limit Minimum: : 21 Years Maximum: 58 Years at the time of sanction Age of Borrower plus repayment period should not exceed retirement age or 60 years of age, whichever is lower. 9 Repayment Period For Category A Salary Account with Bank of Maharashtra - 84 months Salary Account with Other Bank - 60 months For Category B & C 60 months 10 Rate of Interest Click here to view the Interest Rate 11 Deduction For Category A Not to Exceed 65% of the Gross Monthly Income including Proposed EMI. 3 Purpose of loan To cater to the requirements of meeting personal expenses. 4 Eligibility Borrowers are categorized in three category based on employment. Category –A. – Confirmed Employees of Central Govt. / State Govt. / Public Sector Undertakings/ Govt. Educational Institutions having Salary Account with BOM or any other Bank. Satisfactory account relationship with our Bank or any other Bank. Category –B. – Confirmed Employees of Private / Public Limited Company having external rating “A” & above having Salary Account with BOM or any other Bank. Satisfactory salary account relationship with Bank for at least -6- months. Category C. – Other Salary account holders (Confirmed Employees) whose salary is credited in our Bank and tie up arrangement with employer or irrevocable undertaking from employer is available. 5 Min Annual Income Minimum annual Income – 3.00 Lakhs. Minimum past 1 year ITR/Form 16 is Mandatory from current employer. 6 Maximum Quantum of Finance Maximum Rs 20.00 Lakhs. Loan amount is 20 times of Gross Monthly Income or as per Maximum Quantum of Finance whichever is lower. 7 Margin Nil 8 Age Limit Minimum: : 21 Years Maximum: 58 Years at the time of sanction Age of Borrower plus repayment period should not exceed retirement age or 60 years of age, whichever is lower. 9 Repayment Period For Category A Salary Account with Bank of Maharashtra - 84 months Salary Account with Other Bank - 60 months For Category B & C 60 months 10 Rate of Interest Click here to view the Interest Rate 11 Deduction For Category A Not to Exceed 65% of the Gross Monthly Income including Proposed EMI. 4 Eligibility Borrowers are categorized in three category based on employment. Category –A. – Confirmed Employees of Central Govt. / State Govt. / Public Sector Undertakings/ Govt. Educational Institutions having Salary Account with BOM or any other Bank. Satisfactory account relationship with our Bank or any other Bank. Category –B. – Confirmed Employees of Private / Public Limited Company having external rating “A” & above having Salary Account with BOM or any other Bank. Satisfactory salary account relationship with Bank for at least -6- months. Category C. – Other Salary account holders (Confirmed Employees) whose salary is credited in our Bank and tie up arrangement with employer or irrevocable undertaking from employer is available. 5 Min Annual Income Minimum annual Income – 3.00 Lakhs. Minimum past 1 year ITR/Form 16 is Mandatory from current employer. 6 Maximum Quantum of Finance Maximum Rs 20.00 Lakhs. Loan amount is 20 times of Gross Monthly Income or as per Maximum Quantum of Finance whichever is lower. 7 Margin Nil 8 Age Limit Minimum: : 21 Years Maximum: 58 Years at the time of sanction Age of Borrower plus repayment period should not exceed retirement age or 60 years of age, whichever is lower. 9 Repayment Period For Category A Salary Account with Bank of Maharashtra - 84 months Salary Account with Other Bank - 60 months For Category B & C 60 months 10 Rate of Interest Click here to view the Interest Rate 11 Deduction For Category A Not to Exceed 65% of the Gross Monthly Income including Proposed EMI.                

Maha Bank Personal Loan scheme for Salaried customers
Particulars
Scheme guidelines
Name of the scheme
MAHA BANK PERSONAL LOAN SCHEME- for Salaried customers
Type of Facility
Term Loan
Purpose of loan
To cater to the requirements of meeting personal expenses.
Eligibility
Borrowers are categorized in three category based on employment.
Category –A. –
Confirmed Employees of Central Govt. / State Govt. / Public Sector Undertakings/ Govt. Educational Institutions having Salary Account with BOM or any other Bank. Satisfactory account relationship with our Bank or any other Bank.
Category –B. –
Confirmed Employees of Private / Public Limited Company having external rating “A” & above having Salary Account with BOM or any other Bank. Satisfactory salary account relationship with Bank for at least -6- months.
Category C. –
Other Salary account holders (Confirmed Employees) whose salary is credited in our Bank and tie up arrangement with employer or irrevocable undertaking from employer is available.
Min Annual Income
Minimum annual Income – 3.00 Lakhs.
Minimum past 1 year ITR/Form 16 is Mandatory from current employer.
Maximum Quantum of Finance
Maximum Rs 20.00 Lakhs.
Loan amount is 20 times of Gross Monthly Income or as per Maximum Quantum of Finance whichever is lower.
Margin
Nil
Age Limit
Minimum:
: 21 Years
Maximum:
58 Years at the time of sanction
Age of Borrower plus repayment period should not exceed retirement age or 60 years of age, whichever is lower.
Repayment Period
For Category A
Salary Account with Bank of Maharashtra
- 84 months
Salary Account with Other Bank -
60 months
For Category B & C
Rate of Interest
Click here to view the
Interest Rate
Deduction
Not to Exceed 65% of the Gross Monthly Income including Proposed EMI.
Not to Exceed 60% of the Gross Monthly Income including Proposed EMI.
Security
Nil (Clean Loan)
Guarantor
Not required
Processing Fee
1.00 % of the loan amount + GST (Min: Rs 1000/-)
Documentation charge
0.20% of the loan amount + GST
Calculate EMI

Interest Rates
